<Time>1469858111817<//Time><rating>5<//rating>< Text>
II started coming here in 2006 and I've never looked back. Let's be real!! No one remembers their first smog, I mean to be honest everyone hates getting their car smogged, California sucks! When I came to fast smog it was a little bit different......Just a little! I mean getting my car smogged still sucked, but the smog tech Erik who serviced my car made it much better than any of my previous experiences. When they say fast they mean it, my car was done in 10 minutes which was amazing which kept me coming back for years. I purchased a new vehicle a few year ago which allowed me to skip the process for some time. When the lovely state of California notified me I had to get my new car checked out I went back to Fast Smog, to my surprise Erik was still working there. The whole experience was exactly how I remembered, the place was clean, he got me in and out, and even gave me a deal based on a local promotion that had been running even though I didn't have a coupon. All in all the experience was great, and although no one wants to get their car smogged when I have to I will go to Fast Smog in Campbell. Ask for Erik if he still works there.< /Text>

I am a new business owner. I opted to use Minuteman Press after an array of online print shops provided confusing and misleading pricing information, garbled my orders, and/or provided proofs of products that were incorrect or inadequate to address my needs.

The staff at Minuteman Press, Sand Creek Rd, Brentwood instantly swept away the new business owner chaos I was feeling and were attentive as they  listened to my uncertain explanations of the products I required to launch my company. The whole staff brainstormed ideas with me and made suggestions. And then they allowed me countless revisions and proofs of their work prior to printing my order. The combined cost of the products I received from M.M. Press was far less than the total price the online retailers were trying to charge me; and I received a far higher quality product in which every detail was perfected before it was printed. I was married this past April and had trouble finding exactly what I wanted for my wedding invitations. I spent a few months looking everywhere you could imagine- online, in bridal stores, etc. and could not find something simple enough but with the romantic and elegant feel. I had heard of Minuteman for business cards and more corporate products but never heard anything about wedding invitations. They are right around the corner from my house so I decided to walk in and see if they could work with me to make what I had in mind. I am so happy I decided to walk in as I had my invitations made here and they were exactly what I wanted and for half the price of anything else compared online. <Text>I've owned a home in Graeagle Meadows for over 17 years...sadly, I just sold it! But I think I am well qualified to review Graeagle Meadows Golf Course. First - it's a very beautiful and scenic golf course. Second - it's plenty challenging for this 15-handicap...especially from the tips! Third - it's walker-friendly, which is very important to me. Fourth - the clubhouse has excellent food. I have always loved their breakfast. We've gone there for breakfast many, many times when we weren't there for the golf. It's that good. Fifth - it's reasonably priced. Not cheap, but certainly an excellent value for money. Go there, play this course and enjoy the beautiful, small American town of Graeagle while you're there. You won't be disappointed.< /Text>< Name>
Jeffrey 2016Rubicon< /Name>

I wanted to do something special for my friends 60th birthday, and Teatro Martini was a fantastic way to celebrate her birthday. This show was so entertaining. It had comedy, music, magic and amazing talent! Also the food was so delicious! As we  waited to be seated before the show, there were appetizers in a waiting area. < text>
I guess the term  "most outstanding live entertainment" as indicated on their website, is a huge overstatement if you have really experienced quality entertainment. The quality of the show was very lacking. The cast was so so. The costumes were cheap. Only good part was the silk ropes aerealist.
The 4 course meal consisted of a barely warm tomato soup, a house salad,mushy vegetables, overseasoned butterflied chicken and soggy shrimp. For dessert, a brownie like any. All frozen microwaved food.
Cramped lobby where people stand in line for whatever those fritters with ranch sauce were. Expensive drinks full of fillers.
The fact that when I called their customer service number, I got an automated recording from Pirates Adventure, should have been the give away. If Medieval Times is your idea of "outstanding live entertainment", then you won't be disappointed. Otherwise, use your money for a nice meal anywhere else. Even the Outback steakhouse across the street would be a better option.< /text>

< Review>
Highly recommend! Grown up fun! Leave the kids (anyone under 18 give or take a year or two) with the babysitter/at home. Audience participation. Great cocktails, yummy food, & fantastic service!
At the end of the night my cheeks hurt from smiling/laughing so much.
There's no cursing but if you're easily offended this may not be the place for you. Check out a few videos to get an idea, buy tickets on Groupon, & show up approximately 30+ minutes early. First come first seated. Relatively small place so just about any seat will be a good one. The best seats have a clear view of the main stage which will be to your left when you walk in.<//Review>

Teatro Martini is a fun interactive vaudeville style variety show at the Pirates Dinner Theater location. It is definitely adult only and a little racy, but a lot of fun for a night out. As they say, "If you are easily offended, this is probably not the show for you."  I have been a couple times now. The cast and acts change out, so its not the exact same show every time.
The dinner on Saturday night is good. The Thursday, Friday, Sunday shows are better for drinks and appetizers, but they do have a full menu available if you want. Get there early, on Saturday they have appetizers and always have a full bar available before the show.
Check your favorite deal site for tickets, and tip your waitress as she may be singing and dancing as well.</review>

117432080898785407408<//user>
<username>Audrey Zimmerman<//username><Time>1535488122642<//Time><rating>2</rating>< Text>
My advice to you can be stated in two words: arrive early.

I found a Groupon that had decent prices for these tickets and thought it'd be a fun thing to get dressed up for and take my husband to for his birthday. I called ahead to reserve a table and got us the "Night to Remember" upgrade.

They tell you that the doors open at 7:15 and that you should arrive early to check-in. We arrived at 7:00, and found the parking lot totally full. Teatro Martini shares the lot with the Pirates Adventure show. The Pirates show starts first, so all the spaces were taken up by patrons of that show, many of them parked rather badly, so 1/3 of the spaces in the lot, were actually open spots that people parked over the line on.

We had dressed to the nines, because the site said "semi-formal" dress code. I argued with my husband because he wanted to wear a nice pair of converse and I forced him to wear dress shoes. When we arrived, we saw a lot of casual dress and a lot of sneakers. So now I owe my husband one...

When we got in, we took a cute photo and I decided to upgrade our meals again to include the lobster tail. The lovely woman in the gift shop told me to keep my receipt and give it to my server. We got some drinks and Teatro Martini actually provided a small happy hour with some snacks before the show.

We were seated in the back left corner, right by the entrance and literally in front of the manager's table. Our server was Lauren, she was a peach, a lovely lady who tried her very best. But unfortunately, they gave her way too many tables. She was running around her gigantic section and our table didn't get any water until after our first course arrived. I gave Lauren my receipt for the lobster tail upgrade, but she either erroneously put the order in, or the cooks forgot. Because the birthday boy didn't get a lobster tail. When his lobster FINALLY came out, he couldn't eat it because Madame Gretta had come over to say happy birthday to him, as per the "Night to Remember" package I purchased. They offered us two drinks for the lobster tail mistake.

At the end of the show, we left immediately and tried to grab our pictures, but the guy who was standing there got hostile when I asked him for our photo. He kept saying, "It's $20 for the photo." as I was pointing to our printed shot. I said, "But we have the Night to Remember package?" he either ignored me, or didn't hear me, as he was chatting with his colleague. I repeated myself, loudly, and he shoved the photo into my hands without apology.

The service and the way we were treated, given the price tag of it all, is why I'm giving them only 2 stars. I literally sat IN FRONT of the management and they couldn't be half-assed to even look at us or notice that we didn't have any water.

The only saving grace, is that the performance was decent, our server Lauren was incredibly sweet, and the food was actually really good.< /Text>

< text>
Teatro Martini is not what I would call a cabaret style show, itâ€™s a simple and uninspiring sophomoric variety show. How the â€œTeatroâ€ name is associated with this show is beyond me. . . . .
Having twice experienced Teatro Zinzani in 2012, I assumed Teatro Martini would be just as entertaining and delightful and I wanted to love it. Wrong. . . . For starters, the room setup isn't conducive for the size of the crowd, meaning not every seat provides full view of the entire show. We were in group B (out of A, B, C) and were sat on the far end of a table on the extreme right side of the stage. Needless to say we missed out on a number of things because our view was limited. Having the knowledge that the website states that they will make seating adjustments upon request, this is not the case as I did request better seats only to be told that our seats were fine and that we could see the entire show from our locale. Group C had much better seats than those in Group B who sat at my table. When making the reservations I was told seating would be on a first come first served basis and the earlier the arrival the better the seats. Not the case.
The food quality doesn't compare with that of Teatro Zinzani. We had the chicken and salmon. The house served dinner with the first dish brought out being the brisket followed by the chicken. After receiving our chicken dish we waited a good 20 minutes before our salmon was served, and when it arrived it smelled like it had laid up on the bank of a river in the sun before making its way on to our table. The taste matched the stench. While the chicken wasn't great, it was at least edible.
Save your money and put it towards something of value, as Teatro Martini is so incredibly overpriced in comparison to the level and quality of food and entertainment.</text>

<Resp>None</Resp><text>Took my parents and 5 others (party of 8) as part of my mother's birthday celebrations (she turned 87)!  Both of my parents really enjoyed the food, just don't expect a gourmet meal and you won't be disappointed.  The party sampled each of the dinner selections (beef brisked, roasted chicken and salmon) as well as the lobster tail upgrades with a glass of champagne...All acceptable although could have been a bit warmer when served.

Make sure that you arrive early and order drinks from the bar as soon as you enter...if not the line/wait can get a bit long and you might miss out on the appetizers.  All of the appetizers were very tasty.

As other reviewers have mentioned, take the photo when you arrive...you aren't obligated to purchase any copies.  We did and weren't disappointed with the results (we purchased the souvenir copy for $20).

I should mention that we had just returned from our birthday celebration trip to Las Vegas where we saw a CIrque cabaret show "Zumanity" and had two very expensive dinners (chef's table at Gallagher's Steakhouse and at Mastro's Ocean Club) so we are no strangers to fine dining and Cabaret / Live theater.

The show at Teatro Martini was just as entertaining (if you don't expect a XXX rated show) and the food was acceptable at a FRACTION of the price!  My parents enjoyed the show more than the Cirque show and the entertainment (and view) was just as good as our most expensive seats at the Las Vegas theater!

The aerial performer was outstanding (a former Cirque artist; very beautiful as well) and the magician was very entertaining and amazing, especially when you consider both his repartee  and his singing voice!  One in our party is a magician and he enjoyed the act without reservation!

The hostess / MC / diva was excellent as were all of the performers / ensemble!

Our server "Taylor" was both efficient and beautiful!

Don't forget to tip on the full value of your dinner...the performers and your server work very hard to entertain you and they do an outstanding job!< /text>< date>

<Review>Come wizz mee, to zee Teatro Martini

$30 off promo

Boob jokes, penis jokes, vagina jokes your thing?  Then, you're at the right place!  Teatro Martini is a dinner cabaret with a variety of acts & a full course meal (choice of certified Angus braised beef brisket, .chicken leg quarter or center cut salmon filet).  I'm assuming there are accommodations for vegetarians, but nothing specific on the menu or on the website.  The show's kinda bawdy, kinda raunchy, sophomoric if you will - all in good fun & nothing explicit.  Just not family-friendly entertainment.  I arrived in my purple long sleeve collar shirt (more on this later) ready for whatever the night brings.

Teatro Martini is conducted in the same building as Pirate's Dinner Adventure.  The ticket windows have 1 line for each respectively.  Inside, guests are led to the area around the bar & the Pirate's gift shop.  Have your pic professionally taken & buy it later for the reasonable price of $15.

Tray passed appetizers made the rounds, of which I helped empty.

Tonight's dinner-

Tomato bisque
Salad
Certified Angus braised beef brisket-
A generous cut, the brisket was the most tender pot roast I've had.  The best part being the juicy fat, it was laid on a bed of mashed potatoes w/ carrots.

Cheesecake-
The menu said tiramisu, but we were greeted with slices of rich cheesecake.  I suppose tiramisu season is over at the the moment ;p  Regardless, the slice of cheesecake was creamy & a satisfying end to a meal.

The show was a hodgepodge of singing, awe-inspiring acrobatics, comedy, magic, quick change artists and musical revues, interspersed with servings of the night's meals.  I became part of the act on not 1, but 2 occasions.  Wanda picked me out of the audience for the "Rio" segment, saying she liked purple. I then began to shimmy like a maniac, doing a mighty fine job if you ask me, with her and the "Jewels".   Also, I took part in the musical finale, where I once again shook what my mama gave me to hit dance songs from throughout the years.  I was jokingly telling fellow guests that I'm actually an employee at Teatro Martini, and it was all part of the act ;p

Seating is in half circles from the stage for Sections A-C, with booths towards the back.  Within each section is your assigned table, but it's first come, first serve as to which seat you'd like to sit at.

Service was good.  The fair women were quick with bringing out food, drinks and what not.  Parking is in a private lot, shared with Pirate's Dinner Adventure.  Free self parking, and valet is $6.  The self parking is ridiculously close & valet is ludicrously unnecessary.

Personally, I would NOT pay for full price, but like Medieval Times & Teatro Martini's sister show, Pirate's, special promotions are available on a regular basis.

I had a blast! A great time, indeed.  Most assuredly, it's not for everyone, but if you can be open-minded and enjoy some perverted humor, permeated with great singing, dancing, comedy and other entertainment, then I think you're in for a real treat.  Granted, I managed to be part of the extravaganza a couple times, which factored into my enjoyment  level, but I nonetheless enjoyed a fun evening of dinner & an amusing show.

Highly recommend!<//Review><Name>Rodney S< /Name>< Resp>

<time>1617980590666</time><rate>5</rate><Text>To me, this little course is a great value for the So Cal area. Its not very long (just under a 1k yds), but its tricky enough to be worthwhile. There is some decent elevation changes for a course so short. The greens are TINY so accuracy is key. The greens surface is okay, its not a great type of grass for greens. But they probably run fine when not punched and divots repaired (greens seemed to be punched a few weeks ago). It does not have a driving range but it does have a putting green. It also has a small clubhouse that offers refreshments. The only drawback is that you are hitting off of mats at each tee box. But, I guess that's the greens fee trade off. Its nestled in the southwest corner of Ford park. Its bordered by the soccer/baseball fields (currently under construction), the river bed, and a nursery. So it was super quiet during my round. I didn't play very well and was able to finish in under an hour. Although, that was likely more related to my start time. By the time I finished, multiple groups had shown up. So starting at that time would have resulted in at least 1.75 hr round. Awesome little value and great practice opportunity!</Text>< pics>
